  (: Nat Type)

;;;; Define <=
  (: <= 
    (-> $a $a Bool))

    (<= $x $y)

;;;; Define cast functions between Nat and Number
  (: fromNumber 
    (-> Number Nat))
  (= 
    (fromNumber $n) 
    (if 
      (<= $n 0) Z 
      (S (fromNumber (- $n 1)))))
  (: fromNat 
    (-> Nat Number))
  (= 
    (fromNat Z) 0)
  (= 
    (fromNat (S $k)) 
    (+ 1 
      (fromNat $k)))
